 ) rangapanchami, holi ke thik paanch din baad caitra maas kii krishna panchami ko manaai jaati he
 This time Rangpanchami will be celebrated on 6 March
 yah parv khaastaur se maharashtra, gujarat or madhya pradesh main manaaya jaataa he
 In some other parts of the country too, people celebrate it with pomp
 rangapanchami holi kaa hi ek bhaag he
 The festival of Holi runs from Krishna Pratipada to Panchami of the month of Chaitra
 krishna panchami ke din bhi log gulaal se dekhte hai
 Hence it is called Rang Panchami
 rang panchami kokan kshetra kaa khaas tyohaar he
 People believe that the gods are attracted to different colors by blowing colors in the air and applying each other
 isse vaataavaran brahmad main sakaaratmak tanragon kaa sanyog banataa he or rang kanon main sambandhit devataaon ke sparsh kii anubhuti hoti he
 It is believed that on this day flying in the atmosphere, Gulal fills positive qualities in the person and destroys negativity
 vaastu main ishan kone he kya, jiskaa zikr modi ne apane bhaashan main kiya?manyataon ke anusaar vyakti ke andar raj or tam gun hote hai jo nakaaratmak urja utpann karte hai
 On this day people take out colorful processions throughout the city
 rang panchami par ek vishesh prakaar kaa meetha pakwaan bhi gharon main banaaya jaataa he
 Which is called Puranpoli
 faldaayi he caitra maas, aise karen puja-upasnaholi brahmad ke tej kaa utsav he
 Various colors in the universe are realized according to the requirement by traveling through various Tejotsava waves and create a complementary and nutritious environment for the work of the respective component
 is din vayumandal main udaae jane vaale vibhinn rangon ke rang kanon kii ore vibhinn devataaon ke tatv aakarshith hote hai
 The deity blesses the creature by sensing the touch of the deity through the combination of positive waves acting in the universe

 shav kaa postmortem karaayaa ja rahaa he

 " a Spice Jet aircraft going from Hyderabad to Hyderabad with 70 passengers was diverted to Bangalore due to an engine malfunction
 airline ke sutron ne kaha ki udaan esji 1048 bhar rahe bombardier kyuu-400 ke payalton ko cockpit panel par ingine main kharabi hone ke sanket mili, jiske baad bengalooru hawaii adde par vimaan ko land karaane kaa faisla kiya gaya
 Airport officials said all emergency services, including the fire brigade and ambulances, were kept ready so that the aircraft could land safely
 vimaan utarane ke baad yatriyon ko ek anya udaan se haidarabad bheja gaya
 The father of a teenager who lost his life after being pushed after being molested in a moving bus in Moga, Punjab, accepted the Punjab government's compensation and employment offer and agreed to post mortem and the funeral of the deceased's body
 iske baad ghatana ko lekar chaar din se chalaa aa rahaa virodh samaapt ho gaya or kishori kaa antim sanskaar kar diya gaya
 The body of the teenager was cremated at around 8
35 pm on Sunday night in his village Landeke amid tight security
 mukhaagni uske pita ne di, jinhone kaha ki gatirodh dur karne ke liye rajya sarkaar se koi samjhauta nahin hua
 Facing embarrassment and criticism over the incident in Moga on Wednesday, Chief Minister Parkash Singh Badal met the deceased's father and other family members in the evening and spent about 30 minutes with them
 badal ne ghatana ko 'asahneeya' or 'peedaadaayi' bataaya, jabaki police ne kaha ki chaaron aropiyon ko giraftaar kar liya gaya he
 The father of the deceased told reporters, 'I want to insist that i want to cremate my daughter
 ' unhone yah bhi kaha ki vah bina kisi dabaav ke, postmortem karaane ke liye sahamat hue
 The teenager's father was refusing to perform her last rites, stating that he would not cremate his daughter until a case was registered against Deputy Chief Minister Sukhbir Singh Badal and others from Orbit Aviation
 peedit ke pita ne orbit aviation bas seva kaa license radd karne kii maang bhi kii thi
 Sukhbir is one of the owners of this bus company
 kishori ke pita apni maang par jor dene ke liye kuch sthaneey raajnneetigyon ke saath dharne par baithe the
 He said, 'I accept what the state government has offered to us
 unhone (rajya sarkaar ne) hamaari maangen puri kin or aashwaasan diya ki meri beti ke hatyaron ko sajaa di jaaegi
 ' kshatipurti ke bare main unhone kaha ki unhen raashi ke bare main pataa nahin he
 'I cannot say how much compensation there is
 jo bhi mujhe diya ja rahaa he vah mere liye paryaapt he
 i am glad that i will be leaving here with my daughter
 ' Earlier, the government had offered a compensation of Rs 20 lakh and a job for the injured mother, her free treatment zone and also said that the case would be heard in a fast track court
 lekin peedit ke parivaar ne peshkash thukraa di thi
 The comments moga ke upayukta parminder singh gil ne kaha ki jila prashasan ke bajaay bas kii maalik company orbit aviation peedit parivaar ko 24 lakh rupee kaa muaavja degi
 The amount will be deposited in Red Cross Moga from where it will be given to the affected family
 ladki ke pita ne ghatana ko lekar jari virodh khatm bhi karnaa chaha
 'this protest must end
 meri beti kii pehle hi maut ho chuki he

 main ab saamaanya jivan jeena chahta hum
